	scout_car_equipment = {
		year = 1936

		is_archetype = yes
		is_buildable = no
		is_convertable = yes
		picture = archetype_light_tank_equipment
		type = armor
		group_by = archetype

		interface_category = interface_category_armor

		can_be_produced = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = BUL_army_restrictions
				has_idea = HUN_treaty_of_trianon
			}
		}
		#Misc Abilities
		maximum_speed = 8
		reliability = 0.78
		max_strength = 0.5

		#Defensive Abilities
		defense = 5
		breakthrough = 20
		hardness = 0.3
		armor_value = 5

		#Offensive Abilities
		soft_attack = 15
		hard_attack = 2
		ap_attack = 4
		air_attack = 0

		#Space taken in convoy
		lend_lease_cost = 0.2

		build_cost_ic = 8
		fuel_consumption = 1.0
		resources = {
			steel = 2
			rubber = 1
			coal = 4
		}

		module_slots = {
			main_armament_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_tiny_main_armament
				}
			}
			turret_type_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_tiny_turret_type
				}
			}
			engine_type_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_tiny_engine_type
				}
			}
			suspension_type_slot = {
				required = yes
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_suspension_type
				}
			}

			special_type_slot_1 = {
				required = no
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_special_module
					tank_radio_module
				}
			}

			special_type_slot_2 = {
				required = no
				allowed_module_categories = {
					tank_special_module
				}
			}
		}
		default_modules = {
			main_armament_slot = empty
			turret_type_slot = empty
			engine_type_slot = empty
			suspension_type_slot = empty
			#special_type_slot_1 = armour_piercing
			special_type_slot_1 = empty
			special_type_slot_2 = empty
		}
		module_count_limit = { category = tank_radio_module count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { category = tank_secondary_turret count < 2 }
		#module_count_limit = { module = amphibious_drive count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = tank_crew_radios count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = smoke_launchers count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = rangefinder count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = stabilizer count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = assisted_turret_drive count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = auto_loader count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = wet_ammo_storage count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = easy_maintenance count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = additional_machine_guns count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = armor_skirts count < 2 }
		module_count_limit = { module = cutting_corners count < 2 }
	}
